<script>
(function() {
  var bookmarks = document.querySelector('.FilterMenu li.MyBookmarks');
  if (bookmarks) bookmarks.classList.add('SpCog');
  var thanked = document.querySelector('.FilterMenu li.Thanked a');
  if (thanked) {
    var count = thanked.querySelector('span');
    count.outerHTML = '<span class="Aside"><span class="Count">' + count.innerHTML.trim() + '</span></span>';
    var span = document.createElement('span');
    thanked.firstChild.nodeValue = ' ' + thanked.firstChild.nodeValue;
    thanked.insertBefore(span, thanked.firstChild);
    span.outerHTML = '<span aria-hidden="true" class="Sprite SpComments SpThanked"></span>';
  }
})();
</script>
